country_event = { #사천 대기근 컨트리이벤트
	id = china_wr.10
	title = china_wr.10.t
	desc = china_wr.10.d
	picture = GFX_great_famine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.10.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 753
					state = 605
					state = 1004
					state = 748
					state = 752
					state = 751
				}
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_the_threat_of_famine }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_Sichuan_Famine_modifier }
		}
		752 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		751 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		753 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		605 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		748 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		1004 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = china_wr.13 days = 10 }
			country_event = { id = china_wr.49 days = 25 }
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_sichuan_famine
		complete_national_focus = CHI_sichuan_famine_focus
		set_country_flag = CHI_sichuan_famine_start_flag
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #중국 입장에서 8대 열강에게 도움 요청하는 이벤트
	id = china_wr.14
	title = china_wr.14.t
	desc = china_wr.14.d
	picture = GFX_great_famine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.14.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = JAP
						original_tag = USA
						original_tag = GER
						original_tag = AUH
						original_tag = SOV
						original_tag = ITA
						original_tag = ENG
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = china_wr.15 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 days = 2 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #열강 입장에서 중국에게 도움 줄지 말지 이벤트
	id = china_wr.15
	title = china_wr.15.t
	desc = china_wr.15.d
	picture = GFX_great_famine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #도움을 준다
		name = china_wr.15.a
		CHI = { country_event = { id = china_wr.16 days = 1 } }
		CHI = { add_to_variable = { help_okay_var = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = JAP }
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = GER }
			}
			AUH = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = AUH }
			}
			USA = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = USA }
			}
			ITA = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ENG }
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = SOV }
			}
			CHI = { country_event = { id = china_wr.18 days = 2 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = { #아시안 원숭이는 아사하는게 이득이다
		name = china_wr.15.b
		CHI = { country_event = { id = china_wr.17 days = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = JAP }
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = GER }
			}
			AUH = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = AUH }
			}
			USA = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = USA }
			}
			ITA = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ITA }
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = ENG }
			}
			SOV = { country_event = { id = china_wr.15 hours = 1 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = SOV }
			}
			CHI = { country_event = { id = china_wr.18 days = 2 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #구호 결과 도출.
	id = china_wr.18
	title = china_wr.18.t
	desc = {
		text = china_wr.18.desc.a #모든 국가 거부
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var = 0 }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = china_wr.18.desc.b #일부 국가 승인
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var > 0 }
			check_variable = { help_okay_var < 7 }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = china_wr.18.desc.c #모든 국가 승인
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var = 7 }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_great_famine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.18.a #모든 국가 거부
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var = 0 }
		}
		set_country_flag = done_help_flag
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china_wr.18.b #4개 미만 국가 승인
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var > 1 }
			check_variable = { help_okay_var < 4 }
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_2
			add_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_3_a
		}
		set_country_flag = done_help_flag
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china_wr.18.c #4개 이상 국가 승인
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var > 4 }
			check_variable = { help_okay_var < 7 }
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_2
			add_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_3_b
		}
		set_country_flag = done_help_flag
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china_wr.18.d #모든 국가 승인
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { help_okay_var = 7 }
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_2
			add_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_3_c
		}
		set_country_flag = done_help_flag
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #사천 대기근 해결됨 이벤트
	id = china_wr.20
	title = china_wr.20.t
	desc = china_wr.20.d
	picture = GFX_great_famine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.20.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_3_c
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_sichuan_famine_3_c
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_4_a
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_sichuan_famine_4_a
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_4_b
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_sichuan_famine_4_b
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_sichuan_famine_4_c
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_sichuan_famine_4_c
		}
		set_country_flag = finally_solve_problem_in_sichan_flag
		set_country_flag = finally_solve_problem_in_sichan_flag_vote
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		complete_national_focus = CHI_prepare_insufficient_election
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = CHI_presidential_election_preparation_category
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = china_wr.73 days = 2 }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 753
					state = 605
					state = 1004
					state = 748
					state = 752
					state = 751
				}
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHI_Sichuan_Famine_modifier }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #2기 중점 첫 이벤트, 옌후이칭이 대담할 후보를 고르는 이벤트
	id = china_wr.21
	title = china_wr.21.t
	desc = china_wr.21.d
	picture = CHI_Yan_Huiqing
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #진보당
		name = china_wr.21.a
		complete_national_focus = CHI_minsheng_junfu
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
						option = HU_SHIH_YOUNG_CHINA_PARTY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
						option = WANG_JINGEWI_KUOMINTANG
					}
				}
				add = -5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #중청당
		name = china_wr.21.b
		complete_national_focus = CHI_minquan_xianzheng
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
						option = CAI_E_PROGRESSIVE_PARTY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
						option = WANG_JINGEWI_KUOMINTANG
					}
				}
				add = -5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #국민당
		name = china_wr.21.c
		complete_national_focus = CHI_beifang_tongyi
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
							option = DEFAULT
						}
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
						option = HU_SHIH_YOUNG_CHINA_PARTY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHI_ai_behavior_presidential_election
						option = CAI_E_PROGRESSIVE_PARTY
					}
				}
				add = -5
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

		}

				set_politics = {

					election_frequency = 48

				}
			}

		}

			ideology = democratic

			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_minsheng_junfu
					has_completed_focus = CHI_minquan_xianzheng
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = north_china_path_flag
			complete_national_focus = CHI_hufa_democracy_victory

		else = {

		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = CHI_minquan_xianzheng
				AND = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_beifang_tongyi

				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = finally_solve_problem_in_sichan_flag_vote

				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic

country_event = { #서북의 국민당으로의 배반
	id = china_wr.75
	title = china_wr.75.t
	desc = china_wr.75.d
	picture = GFX_kuomintag_nono
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.75.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				SIK = { is_subject = no }
			}
			ROOT = { annex_country = { target = SIK transfer_troops = yes } }
			#SIK = { set_cosmetic_tag = SIK_under_KMT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				XSM = { has_cosmetic_tag = XSM_under_CHI }
			}
			XSM = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			ROOT = { annex_country = { target = XSM transfer_troops = yes } }
			#XSM = { set_cosmetic_tag = XSM_under_KMT }
		}
		ROOT = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SIK
						is_core_of = XSM
					}
					NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
				enable_state_integration_60_compliance = yes
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SIK
			}
			remove_core_of = SIK
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = XSM
			}
			remove_core_of = XSM
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

					is_core_of = GSM
					is_core_of = NSM
					is_core_of = ETS
					is_core_of = SHX
					is_core_of = PRC
					is_core_of = NPA
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = SIK
			remove_core_of = XSM
			remove_core_of = GSM
			remove_core_of = NSM
			remove_core_of = ETS
			remove_core_of = SHX
			remove_core_of = PRC
			remove_core_of = NPA
			add_core_of = CHI
		}
		617 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = china_wr.152
	title = china_wr.152.t
	desc = china_wr.152.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.152.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CHI
			}
			add_stability = 0.025
			if = {
				limit = {
					MON = { is_subject_of = CHI }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						TAN = { exists = yes }
					}
					MON = { annex_country = { target = TAN transfer_troops = no } }
				}
				else = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							state = 329
						}
						transfer_state_to = MON
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						TAN = { exists = yes }
					}
					CHI = { annex_country = { target = TAN transfer_troops = no } }
				}
				else = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							state = 329
						}
						transfer_state_to = CHI
					}

		OR = {
			818 = { is_owned_by = CHI }
			MON = { is_subject_of = CHI }

			}
			else = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						state = 329
					}
					transfer_state_to = MON
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					TAN = { exists = yes }
				}
				CHI = { annex_country = { target = TAN transfer_troops = no } }
			}
			else = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						state = 329
					}
					transfer_state_to = CHI
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
				NOT = { has_war_with = MAN }
			}
			CHI = { country_event = { id = china_wr.268 days = 15 } }

		}
		ai_chance = {

		}
	}
}

				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_political_power_factor = 0.05 }

					has_country_flag = china_wr_276_a2
				}
				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_consumer_goods_factor = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.1 }

				limit = {

				}
				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_production_lack_of_resource_penalty_factor = -0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_required_garrison_factor = -0.1 }
				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_industrial_capacity_factory = -0.05 }

				add_to_variable = { CHI_constitution_production_factory_start_efficiency_factor = 0.05 }

country_event = {
	id = china_wr.336
	title = china_wr.336.t
	desc = china_wr.336.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_train
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = china_wr.336.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { CHI_one_one_way_var = 17 }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_20th_century_silk_road_high
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { CHI_one_one_way_var > 13 }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_20th_century_silk_road_middle
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { CHI_one_one_way_var > 8 }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_20th_century_silk_road_middle_low
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { CHI_one_one_way_var > 3 }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_20th_century_silk_road_low
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = CHI_20th_century_silk_road_very_low
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

		is_subject = no
	}
	option = {
		name = china_wr.2001.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_build_arms_factory
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_build_arms_factory
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					free_building_slots = {
						type = arms_factory
						value > 0
						include_locked = no
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_build_civilian_factory
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_build_civilian_factory
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					free_building_slots = {
						type = industrial_complex
						value > 0
						include_locked = no
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_build_dockyard
			}
			clr_country_flag = CHI_build_dockyard
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_coastal = yes
					free_building_slots = {
						type = dockyard
						value > 0
						include_locked = no
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				set_country_flag = CHI_build_arms_factory
			}
			40 = {
				set_country_flag = CHI_build_civilian_factory
			}
			20 = {
				set_country_flag = CHI_build_dockyard
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Self_Reliance_bar_var = 100 }
			}
			country_event = { id = china_wr.2001 days = 80 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Self_Reliance_bar_var > 49 }
			}
			country_event = { id = china_wr.2001 days = 160 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = china_wr.2001 days = 240 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

				add_idea = KMT_national_assembly_legitimacy_low
			}

				remove_idea = KMT_national_assembly_legitimacy_low
				add_idea = KMT_national_assembly_legitimacy_medium
			}
		}
		else_if = {

			}

				remove_idea = KMT_national_assembly_legitimacy_medium

country_event = { #서북 평정
	id = kuomintag_wr.89
	title = kuomintag_wr.89.t
	desc = kuomintag_wr.89.d
	picture = GFX_kuomintag_nono
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = kuomintag_wr.89.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				SIK = { is_subject = no }
			}
			SIK = { country_event = kuomintag_wr.90 }
		}
		XSM = { country_event = kuomintag_wr.90 }
		GSM = { country_event = kuomintag_wr.90 }
		NSM = { country_event = kuomintag_wr.90 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #서북 평정
	id = kuomintag_wr.90
	title = kuomintag_wr.90.t
	desc = kuomintag_wr.90.d
	picture = GFX_kuomintag_nono
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = kuomintag_wr.90.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = SIK }
			}
			SIK = { set_cosmetic_tag = SIK_under_KMT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = XSM }
			}
			XSM = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			XSM = { set_cosmetic_tag = YOU_under_KMT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = NSM }
			}
			GSM = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			NSM = { set_cosmetic_tag = YOU_under_KMT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { original_tag = GSM }
			}
			NSM = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
			GSM = { set_cosmetic_tag = YOU_under_KMT }
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
							has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROOT
						autonomous_state = KMT_autonomy_autonomous_provincial_government
						freedom_level = 0.5
					}
					else = {
						puppet = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = kuomintag_wr_90_tt
		FROM = { country_event = kuomintag_wr.91 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = kuomintag_wr.90.b
		FROM = { country_event = kuomintag_wr.92 }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = kuomintag_wr.119
	title = kuomintag_wr.119.t
	desc = kuomintag_wr.119.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_PRC_he_long_arrives
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = kuomintag_wr.119.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_blue_shirts_society_dlc
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_blue_shirts_society_dlc
				add_idea = KMT_bomilguk_intelligence_spirit_dlc
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_blue_shirts_society_nodlc
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_blue_shirts_society_nodlc
				add_idea = KMT_bomilguk_intelligence_spirit_no_dlc
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_CC_clique_dlc
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_CC_clique_dlc
				add_idea = KMT_bomilguk_intelligence_spirit_dlc
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = KMT_CC_clique_nodlc
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = KMT_CC_clique_nodlc
				add_idea = KMT_bomilguk_intelligence_spirit_no_dlc
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
				add_ideas = KMT_bomilguk_intelligence_spirit_no_before_dlc
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = KMT_bomilguk_intelligence_spirit_no_before_no_dlc
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}
